plane-crazy 2020-04-29 15:30:29 VoxelBox#8950
Suggestion #5251
Please, add more wedges
[Building]

It's been about half a year since we've had a major update that added more wedges to the game. At least it's felt like half a year, I've lost count of how long it's been. I find it very frustrating when I can't build things the way I want because there simply isn't a wedge or method that allows me to build a certain shape. I even find myself abandoning some projects because I literally cannot make the body of a craft to the way it's supposed to look like without having to significantly alter how I build it. So, here's a list of all wedges that I think need to be added:

‚Ä¢ Half wedge variants of all current wedges.
There are still quite a few wedges that don't have their own half wedge variant (wedges2 sub-category).

‚Ä¢ A variant of all half wedges that have the bottom half of the block filled.
Essentially like the half wedge in the wedges sub-category.

‚Ä¢ Longer wedges
We have a 1x7 beam. Why do we still not have a wedge that's longer than 4 blocks?

‚Ä¢ More variants for the corner and triangle wedges
Currently, corner and triangle wedges come in variants that are only 1 block wide. Having more variants of these wedges (like 2x2, 3x3, etc) can help simplify the building process for certain crafts that are very geometric in shape.
